Junior Geophysicist- Fiber-optic Sensing & AI (Fresher)

Tranzmeo
Infopark

Seeking a Junior Geophysicist with Python skills for fiber-optic sensing and AI projects. Responsibilities include data analysis, model building, and field deployments.

0-2 YearsPythonFiber-optic SensingGeophysics
Apply by: 02 Oct 2025

Junior Geophysicist - Fiber-optic Sensing & AI (Fresher)

We are seeking a motivated Junior Geophysicist (recent graduate) to dive into projects involving Distributed Acoustic Sensing (DAS), fiber‑optic sensor data, and Python‑driven AI analysis. You’ll work closely with geophysicists, data scientists, and engineers to drive data‑centric insights and support field deployments.

Key Responsibilities

  • Support data acquisition, preprocessing, and interpretation from fiber‑optic sensing systems (DAS/DTS).
  • Analyze large time‑series datasets using Python (NumPy, Pandas, SciPy, Matplotlib).
  • Collaborate with AI/ML experts to build models for signal classification, event detection, or anomaly identification.
  • Participate in field activities, including deploying sensors, monitoring systems, and validating datasets.
  • Document workflows, results, and technical insights clearly in reports or code comments.

Required Qualifications

  • Bachelor's or Master's degree in Geophysics, Geoscience, Physics, Engineering, or related discipline.
  • Fundamental understanding of seismic wave behavior and fiber‑optic sensing principles.
  • Basic proficiency in Python and experience with data‑analysis libraries.
  • Interest in machine learning—any exposure to scikit‑learn, TensorFlow, or PyTorch is a plus.
  • Excellent analytical thinking, communication skills, and collaborative mindset.

Preferred (Nice-to-Have)

  • Experience with signal processing, time‑series analysis, or seismic inversion methods.
  • Familiarity with version control systems (e.g., Git) and Jupyter notebooks.
  • Willingness and physical ability to participate in occasional fieldwork and travel.

What You’ll Gain

  • Hands‑on experience at the intersection of geophysics, fiber‑optic sensing, and AI.
  • Mentorship from industry professionals and cross‑disciplinary collaboration.
  • Exposure to real‑world problems in energy, infrastructure, and environmental monitoring.

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at lakshmi@team.tranzmeo.com

Technical Lead – Linux Administration

HashRoot Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

Seeking a Technical Lead with 7+ years of Linux Administration experience. Responsibilities include managing servers, virtualization, networking, and troubleshooting infrastructure. Requires strong communication skills.

7+ YearsLinux AdministrationProxmox VENetworking
Apply by: 30 Nov 2025

Technical Lead – Linux Administration

Location: Hybrid Employment Type: Full-Time Experience Required: 7+ years (or less with equivalent skill set)

We are seeking an experienced and highly skilled Technical Lead (Linux Administration) to join our team. The ideal candidate will have deep expertise in Linux server administration, virtualization platforms, networking fundamentals, and system troubleshooting. This role involves leading technical initiatives, supporting infrastructure, and collaborating with cross-functional teams to ensure seamless operations.

Key Responsibilities

Linux Administration - Install, configure, and maintain all major Linux distributions (Debian, Ubuntu, CentOS, RHEL, Fedora, SUSE, Arch). - Manage partitioning, file systems (ext4, XFS, Btrfs, ZFS), and package management tools (APT, YUM/DNF, Zypper, Pacman). - Handle system initialization using systemd and init.d.

User & Permission Management - Manage users, groups, and sudoers access. - Configure file ownership, ACLs, and security frameworks such as SELinux and AppArmor.

Virtualization & Hosting - Install, configure, and manage Proxmox VE. - Create, manage, and monitor KVM virtual machines & LXC containers. - Implement backup and restore strategies within Proxmox. - Integrate networking and storage solutions (Ceph, ZFS, NFS, iSCSI). - Provide support for WHMCS-based help desk solutions.

Networking Fundamentals - Administer and troubleshoot TCP/IP, DNS, DHCP, NAT, VLANs, and VPNs. - Manage IP addressing, subnetting, and routing. - Configure and maintain firewalls (iptables, nftables, firewalld, ufw). - Conduct network diagnostics using tools like ping, traceroute, netstat, ss, tcpdump, and nmap.

Content Delivery Networks (CDN) - Understand CDN concepts and work with CDN providers. - Integrate websites/services with CDN and configure DNS for CDN usage.

Troubleshooting & Maintenance - Resolve OS-level issues including boot/GRUB problems, service failures, and resource bottlenecks. - Analyze logs (/var/log, rsyslog, journald) and diagnose hardware issues (SMART monitoring, RAID, NIC failures, memory/CPU diagnostics). - Use remote management tools (iLO, iDRAC, IPMI). - Coordinate with onsite teams for cabling, hardware replacements, and device setup; manage escalation procedures and maintain documentation.

Monitoring & Security - Implement and maintain monitoring tools (Nagios, Zabbix, Prometheus, Grafana). - Harden servers by configuring firewalls, securing SSH, and applying timely patches.

Qualifications & Skills

  • 7+ years of Linux Administration experience (or equivalent skill set).
  • Strong knowledge of virtualization platforms (Proxmox, KVM, LXC).
  • Solid understanding of networking, firewalls, and CDN integration.
  • Proven experience in troubleshooting at OS and hardware levels.
  • Familiarity with monitoring tools and security best practices.
  • Excellent communication and coordination skills for working with onsite teams.

Preferred Attributes

  • Certification(s) in Linux Administration, Networking, or Virtualization (RHCE, LFCS, CompTIA Linux+, etc.).
  • Hands-on experience with WHMCS or similar help desk systems.
  • Ability to document processes and create clear technical instructions.

Contact: Interested candidates please share your resume at careers@hashroot.com. If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at careers@hashroot.com.

Ideal Candidate Profile

  • Proficiency with Tailwind CSS, utility-first styling, responsive design, and theming.
  • Proven experience writing unit tests and E2E tests (Jest, Playwright or equivalent).
  • Solid grasp on REST APIs, concurrency, locking / session management, and distributed systems fundamentals.

  • Strong software architecture sense, modular design, clean code practices, and ability to reason about scaling.

Nice-to-Haves

  • Knowledge of Azure Key Vault, Azure API Management (APIM), or API lifecycle tools.
  • Experience in CI/CD pipelines, automated deployments, cloud-native architectures.
  • Past work on collaborative or multi-user real-time applications (CRDTs, OT, conflict resolution).
  • Familiarity with distributed locks, Redis, or similar concurrency tooling.

FLUTTER DEVELOPER at SMARTHMS & SOLUTIONS (P) Ltd

Company: SMARTHMS & SOLUTIONS (P) Ltd Location: Technopark Phase 1, Trivandrum, Kerala, 695581 Website: https://shmsolutions.in

Contact Email: careers@shmsolutions.in

Job Published: September 29, 2025 Closing Date: November 13, 2025

Brief Description

SMARTHMS & SOLUTIONS (P) Ltd is seeking a Flutter Developer with 1 to 3 years of experience to join their team.

Job Responsibilities

  • Develop mobile applications using the Flutter framework and Dart programming language.
  • Work with designers to create user-friendly and visually appealing interfaces.
  • Test and fix issues in the application code to ensure it works properly.
  • Optimize the performance of the app, including reducing size and improving speed.
  • Collaborate with other team members, such as designers and backend developers.
  • Use version control systems, like Git, to manage code and collaborate with others.
  • Document code, processes, and project requirements for future reference.
  • Stay updated with the latest trends and advancements in mobile app development.

Preferred Skills

  • Proficient in Flutter framework and Dart programming language.
  • Knowledge of mobile app development principles and best practices.
  • Familiarity with front-end technologies like HTML, CSS, and JavaScript.
  • Understanding of UI/UX design principles and ability to work with designers.
  • Experience with RESTful APIs and integrating backend services.
  • Familiarity with version control systems, particularly Git.
  • Knowledge of agile development methodologies and collaborative tools.
  • Problem-solving and analytical thinking skills.
  • Good communication and teamwork abilities.

Qualification

  • Bachelors or Master’s degree in computer or related fields.

Salary

  • 35,000 - 40,000 INR per month.

About Spericorn Technology:

Spericorn Technology is a global software development firm dedicated to making a positive impact through technology. We are a team of inquisitive IT professionals with extensive experience in reputable organizations and open-source projects worldwide. We invite you to join our skilled team and help transform ideas into tangible realities. We seek candidates who will uphold our organization's commitment to quality, integrity, and excellence. Our services span various cutting-edge technologies, including blockchain and Artificial Intelligence.

"A team is a group of people who support each other to achieve great results, and we give utmost importance to teamwork."

Role Description:

We are seeking a Lead Full Stack Developer to enhance our organization's capabilities.

Preferred Skills and Responsibilities:

  • Lead and manage a full-stack development team working on the MERN (MongoDB, Express, React, Node.js) stack.
  • Architect, design, and develop scalable and secure applications with a strong focus on performance.
  • Ensure robust backend development using Node.js and solid frontend implementation with React/Next.js.
  • Drive CI/CD processes, version control (Git), and code quality best practices throughout the team.
  • Collaborate closely with clients and stakeholders to gather requirements, provide regular updates, and ensure successful project delivery.
  • Mentor and guide team members to foster technical growth and enhance productivity.
  • Leverage domain expertise, particularly in fintech or related industries.
